sample data transformation:
===========================
{
  var data    = window['__abc_com__']
  var modules = data.page.content.shell.module
  var videos  = []
  var tiles, video, brand, show_id, video_type, video_id, locked

  modules = modules.filter(function(module) {
    return (
         (module.type === 'tilegroup')
      && Array.isArray(module.tiles)
      && module.tiles.length
    )
  })

  for (var i1=0; i1 < modules.length; i1++) {
    tiles = modules[i1].tiles

    tiles = tiles.filter(function(tile) {
      return (
           (tile.type === 'video')
        && (tile.video instanceof Object)
        && (tile.video.id)
        && (tile.video.id.substring(0,4).toLowerCase() === 'vdka')
      )
    })

    for (var i2=0; i2 < tiles.length; i2++) {
      video      = tiles[i2].video
      brand      = video.brand || '001'
      show_id    = ((video.show instanceof Object) && video.show.id)
                    ? video.show.id
                    : '-1'
      video_type = video.type || 'lf'
      video_id   = video.id
      locked     = video.accesslevel && (video.accesslevel !== "0")

      videos.push({
        brand:       brand,
        show_id:     show_id,
        video_type:  video_type,
        video_id:    video_id,
        locked:      locked,
        title:       video.title       || '',
        description: video.description || '',
        duration_ms: video.duration    || 0,
        season:      video.seasonnumber,
        episode:     video.episodenumber
      })
    }
  }

  console.log(JSON.stringify(videos, null, 2))
}

page detection:
===============
{
  var data            = window['__abc_com__']
  var is_episode_list = (data.page.type === 'show')  && (data.page.subType === 'episode-guide')
  var is_episode      = (data.page.type === 'video') && (data.page.subType === 'episode')
  var video, brand, show_id, video_type, video_id, locked, episode, page

  if (is_episode) {
    video      = data.page.content.video.layout.video
    brand      = video.brand || '001'
    show_id    = ((video.show instanceof Object) && video.show.id)
                  ? video.show.id
                  : '-1'
    video_type = video.type || 'lf'
    video_id   = video.id
    locked     = video.accesslevel && (video.accesslevel !== "0")
    episode    = {
      brand:       brand,
      show_id:     show_id,
      video_type:  video_type,
      video_id:    video_id,
      locked:      locked,
      title:       video.title       || '',
      description: video.description || '',
      duration_ms: video.duration    || 0,
      season:      video.seasonnumber,
      episode:     video.episodenumber
    }
  }

  page = {
    is_episode_list: is_episode_list,
    is_episode:      is_episode,
    episode:         episode || null
  }

  console.log(JSON.stringify(page, null, 2))
}
